NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Director  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

Jayasurya Stores, Veerapampalayam Pirivu, Perundurai Road, Erode has been living as Male after undergoing Hormonal Change 
procedure by Dr. Muthukumaran Jayapaul at 5/2, 1st Avenue, Sastri Nagar, Adyar, Chennai and an Elaborate Sex Reassignment 
Surgery at Apollo Cosmetic Clinics, 1st Floor, Plot No. 41/42, 53/54, Sathyadev Avenue, MRC Nagar, R.A. Puram, Chennai
by Dr. Shivaram Bharathwaj MBBS., DNB., General Surgery, FRCS-General Surgery, FRCS-Plastic Surgery.   By this I, may be 
treated as a Male and shall henceforth be known as ADVIK LAVITHRAN.
Erode,
